          <h2 class="c-entry-box--compact__title">
           <a data-analytics-link="article" data-chorus-optimize-field="hed" href="https://www.vox.com/2021/3/8/22319673/derek-chauvin-george-floyd-murder-trial">
            The trial of Derek Chauvin, charged with George Floyd’s death, has been delayed
           </a>
          </h2>
          <p class="p-dek c-entry-box--compact__dek" data-chorus-optimize-field="dek">
           The prosecution has asked to reinstate a third-degree murder charge.
          </p>

          <h2 class="c-entry-box--compact__title">
           <a data-analytics-link="article" data-chorus-optimize-field="hed" href="https://www.vox.com/2021/3/6/22316958/third-stimulus-check-1400-how-much-who-gets-when-to-expect">

           </a>
          </h2>

          <h2 class="c-entry-box--compact__title">
           <a data-analytics-link="feature" data-chorus-optimize-field="hed" href="https://www.vox.com/identities/2021/3/8/22318412/international-womens-day-history-2021-strike">
            The little-known radical history of International Women’s Day
           </a>
          </h2>
          <p class="p-dek c-entry-box--compact__dek" data-chorus-optimize-field="dek">
           International Women’s Day is celebrated with everything from flowers to breakfast. But the holiday started with a 1907 labor strike.
          </p>

    <div class="OUTBRAIN" data-ob-template="Vox.com" data-src="https://www.vox.com/" data-widget-id="AR_8">
    </div>
    <script charset="utf-8" type="text/javascript">
     (function(){
  // load outbrain js
  function loadOutbrain(){
    var ref = document.querySelector("div.OUTBRAIN");

    var script = document.createElement('script');
    script.setAttribute('type','text/javascript');
    script.setAttribute('src', 'https://widgets.outbrain.com/outbrain.js');
    script.setAttribute('async', 'async');

    ref.appendChild(script);
  }

  // Disable on mobile and tablet screens
  // 880px is the upper bound for the `medium` breakpoint defined in UserAgent JS lib.
  var shouldDisable = false && screen.width <= 880;
  var scrollSubscriber = document.cookie.indexOf("scroll0=") > -1;
  var hymnalPreviewContent = !!(window.location.href.indexOf("concert_preview") > -1);

  if (!shouldDisable && !scrollSubscriber && !hymnalPreviewContent) {
    // first, set a timeout to loadOutbrain, in case no ads load in 5s
    // (i.e., blocked). once an ad has loaded, create a new timeout that
    // will load outbrain if openmic doesn't get loaded in 2s
    //
    var adBlockerTimeoutId = setTimeout(loadOutbrain, 5000);
    document.body.addEventListener('first_ad_rendered', function(){
      clearTimeout(adBlockerTimeoutId);
      var outbrainTimeoutId = setTimeout(loadOutbrain, 2000);
      document.body.addEventListener('playlistRendered', function(){
        clearTimeout(outbrainTimeoutId);
      });
    });
  }
})();
    </script>
